To find the total number of pails of water he collects every day, we need to add the number of pails he collects in the morning and the number of pails he collects in the afternoon.\n\nLet's do that:\n\n9558390 (pails in the morning) + 6 (pails in the afternoon) = ?\n\nFirst, we add the two numbers:\n\n9558390 + 6 = 9558396\n\nSo, Baldur collects a total of 9558396 pails of water every day.\n\nSince each pail contains 1 liter of water, we can multiply the total number of pails by 1 to find the total number of liters of water he gets every day:\n\n9558396 pails/day Ã— 1 liter/pail = 9558396 liters/day\n\nFINAL ANSWER: The answer is 9558396."], ['Baldur gets water from a well.
